# PLAN.md — Implementation Roadmap and Status

**This file is the single source of implementation status.** It tells every session
what is done, in progress, blocked, and next. It **references** the
specification in `docs/architecture/` (rule R-4, AGENTS.md) and never restates it:
if you need protocol content, follow the *Spec* column.

How to work this file (full protocol: AGENTS.md):

- Sessions pick **one** milestone: the 🔨 one, else the first ⬜ whose *Depends* are ✅.
- A milestone is ✅ only with green quality gates and a `spec-reviewer` pass without
  blockers (its *Verify* obligations are part of the milestone).
- Update this file **in the same session as the change**: status, *Current focus*,
  and a *Session log* row. Append to logs; never rewrite their history. Dates absolute
  (YYYY-MM-DD).

Legend: ⬜ pending · 🔨 in progress · ✅ done · ⛔ blocked · 🅿 deferred (post-v1)

---

## Current focus

**B9 ✅ (2026-07-16, worktree `milestone-B9`).** The keeper layer exists on both sides of the chain boundary (full inventory in the B9 milestone row). On-chain: the 08 §6.3 keeper meter (two tranches, latch-once alarms + post-exhaustion payment latch, per-epoch reset) resolving SQ-49, the frame-free `KeeperRebateSink` seam, and strictly state-advancing rebate call sites in **every** crank pallet — both reviews' drain vectors (welfare daily-gate re-records, registry file→refund→close farming, paid no-op probes under the pending `()` dispatcher) are closed with regression tests, and the 07 §4 `ack_observed` keeper-class rebate is live. Real USDC payouts ride a narrow `RebatePayout` seam from the `KEEPER__`/`ORACLE__` pots with a try-state custody-drift alarm; everything is fail-soft (a rebate can never affect its crank) and pays 0 until `keeper.rebate` is calibrated (SQ-117, B5). Off-chain: `keeper/bleavit-keeper`, a separate-workspace subxt-dynamic reference keeper — pure tested planner (due-predicates mirror the on-chain guards; absent pallets degrade to disabled roles), race-tolerant nonce-pipelined submitter, 12 §6.3-aligned Prometheus metrics, dry-run, signer-required live mode, operator README. Orchestrated with **Codex subagents (gpt-5.6-sol/xhigh)**: 2 parallel authors → triple review (2× spec-reviewer + adversarial Codex, 2 blockers/7 majors/11 minors combined) → 2 fix rounds + 1 surgical revert (the off-chain review's one major was wrong at the pallet layer — A6's deliberate `FilingCount` guard makes zero-filing epochs unclosable; the keeper must not plan them) → re-review 0/0. SQ-115…SQ-126 logged. Gates green (workspace + keeper workspace + benchmarks/try-runtime legs + no_std + reference-model + doc links). **Next:** the open B1a A8/A11 runtime wiring (binds `InDecisionWindow`, the meter's epoch clock and the epoch/guard rebate seams), B5 (weights incl. registry `WeightInfo=()` + `keeper.rebate` calibration), B6/B7.

**B4 ✅ (2026-07-16, worktree `milestone-B4`).** The XCM layer shipped as `runtime/bleavit-xcm`, a runtime-independent library crate B1a wires (see the B4 milestone row for the full inventory): the 09 §6.1 default-deny rule-table components, the 07 §8 probe with querier authentication + query-id partition + refund-capturing appendix, the 09 §4 coretime funding leg on the **verified relay-teleport route** (V-19 — the spec's reserve-transfer wording would have failed `UntrustedReserveLocation` against the live Coretime config; 09 §4/§6.1 amended), mint-leg-first 09 §5.2 caps, the `pallet_xcm` call classifier (exit pinned to AH; `claim_assets` self-scoped per the amended trapped-assets row), and two new xcm-free seams in `pallet-oracle`/`pallet-futarchy-treasury` (`ProbeDispatch`/`RenewalDispatch`) with ready dispatcher impls — closing the dual review's "the pass paths are unreachable by assembly alone" majors. Orchestrated with **Codex subagents (gpt-5.6-sol/xhigh)**: author → dual review (spec-reviewer 0/3/5 + adversarial Codex **7 blockers/5 majors**) → one remediation round → focused re-pass **all CLOSED, 0 blocker/0 major** (its 4 minors also fixed). V-3/V-6/V-16…V-19 verified; SQ-110…SQ-114 logged; four R-1 doc amendments in the Decision log. Gates green (bleavit-xcm 33 · oracle 75 · treasury 28 · full workspace script · no_std · benchmarks/try-runtime legs · I-24 lint · reference-model 21 · doc links). **Merged onto post-B1a/B2/B3 main in-session** (see the follow-up session-log row): the runtime now wires the two B4 seams, and the PR-review P1s on the renewal leg are fixed. Remaining seam bindings (Params-backed `TraderRates` — needs new 13 keys first, SQ-112 — caps meters SQ-110/SQ-111, health→welfare SQ-113) stay follow-ups.

**B3 ✅ (2026-07-16) — the chain boots.** `node/bleavit-node` (thin `polkadot-omni-node-lib =0.14.1` branding — the runtime rides the chain spec, 02 §11) + the `deploy/` chain-spec pipeline (pinned `chain-spec-builder 17.0.0`; structural validator enforcing the 02 §8 identity, the 02 §10 distinct-peer bootnode thresholds and the full 08 §2.1 genesis-allocation gate) + genesis presets carrying the exact five-group 1B-VIT allocation with `pallet-vesting =46.0.0` founding-team schedules (conservative 0%-at-cliff curve; index 14; D-13 force_* nobody rows). The previously-unbuildable node dependency closure was unblocked by vendoring the fully-yanked `core2 0.4.0` (`[patch.crates-io]`, V-15) + the stable2603-1 maintenance pins. **End-to-end verified: a dev node imports blocks from a freshly generated spec.** Dual review (spec-reviewer + Codex adversarial) — all majors/highs fixed in-session, most notably the deliberate **removal** of a bespoke fee-past-the-vesting-lock adapter (strict "unvested VIT pays no fees" ruling; USDC fee path per 08 §9) and the validator's distinct-peer-ID + genesis gates. 08 §2.1 [VERIFY] resolved; SQ-107…SQ-109 logged for ratification. **Next:** wire A8/A11 into the runtime (the B1a follow-up: Config + pending-seam swap + SQ-96), then **B2** (`FutarchyApi`); B7 (zombienet/chopsticks) is now unblocked by B3.

**B1a ✅ (2026-07-16) — the runtime exists.** `runtime/bleavit-runtime` is now a real Cumulus parachain runtime (`construct_runtime!` over the 10 production pallets A1–A7/A9/A10 + the standard/system/Cumulus set, `frame_executive`, the `CheckMetadataHash`-carrying TxExtension stack, `BaseCallFilter = SafetyFilter<BleavitSafetyClassifier>`, stable2603 `=`-exact pins, genesis presets, `impl_runtime_apis!` — **not** `FutarchyApi`, that's B2), replacing the frame-free B1 composition model. It **builds to Wasm** (`wasm32v1-none`). **A8 (`pallet-epoch`) + A11 (`pallet-execution-guard`) landed on `main` (#56) mid-session** — this runtime holds their documented `construct_runtime!` index slots (61/62) + **G-1 fail-closed pending seam adapters** (authorize/settle/file/report nothing); **wiring the two now-available pallets into the runtime — Config + swapping the pending seams (`PendingA8Authority`/`PendingEpochClock`/`PendingReporting`/`PendingRegistryEpoch`/`PendingGuardian*`/`PendingUpgradeProvider`) + tests — is the immediate follow-up**, kept out of this PR to preserve B1a's reviewed scope. Orchestrated with **Codex subagents** (author → dual review → fix): the dual review's **1 blocker + 1 major + 1 P1 + P2s** and the **PR #57 Codex-bot's 3 findings** were triaged — fixed in-session with regressions: **`sudo.sudo_as` denied** (forges arbitrary `Signed(who)` → impersonates the welfare settlement sovereign / steals VIT; SQ-99), the **floor/ceil-swapped referenda support curves** (would `Perbill::sub`-underflow and brick every values track), the **CONST/entrenched `set_param` values-enactment gap**, **try-runtime error-masking**, **genesis `PhaseFlags`↔sudo-key consistency**, a **latent no_std `Vec`-import defect** in two pallets' `benchmarking.rs`, plus the **bot P2** (`referenda.cancel/kill` added to the values-enactment allowlist) and **bot P1** (the five `ConstitutionalValues` referenda tracks collapsed onto one track — the shared track now uses the **strongest/entrenched thresholds** so no values action can enact below its required bar; full per-track discrimination is the values-layer milestone, SQ-103). The **bot's phase3-cap P1** is an A2-ledger/B4-XCM obligation (09 §5.2 enforces the caps at the ledger split path + XCM inflow leg — **no live inflow path exists in B1a**; SQ-105). **One open blocker routes to B4:** USDC `ForeignAssets` is `u32`-id-1337-keyed (matching every A2/A3/A6 pallet) but 02 §7.4/§8 freeze it XCM-`Location`-keyed (**SQ-101**). No `docs/architecture/` edits — every divergence is fail-closed/stricter-than-spec and logged **SQ-99…SQ-105**. Gates green (fmt · clippy `-D warnings` · workspace suites · runtime tests + try-runtime · release wasm + runtime-benchmarks wasm builds · reference-model 21/21 · doc links). **Next: wire A8/A11 into the runtime; B4 resolves SQ-101; B2 wires `FutarchyApi` over this shell.**

**B1a CI follow-up (2026-07-16, draft PR #59):** CI uses the pinned Rust 1.89.0 toolchain and installs both runtime targets (`wasm32v1-none` preferred, `wasm32-unknown-unknown` fallback). The branch preserves B3's Rust cache and installs its native build dependencies (`libclang-dev` and `protobuf-compiler`). Full workspace gates and the canonical runtime-Wasm build are green.

**Track M (M0–M3) is finished — M1, M2, M3 all ✅ as of 2026-07-15; one PR (`feat/track-m-finish-m1-m2-m3`) carries all three and fully remediates the 2026-07-15 Track M audit.** **M2:** `exp2`/`log2`/`ln` reworked at guarded Q96 precision — **0 ulp over 10⁶ dense-bit points** (was 10.11); per-commit 1,286-point dense-bit single-generator corpus (`tools/fixed` retired, both CSVs gone); exact-u256 domain compare; f64 gated out of `no_std`; real `--no-default-features` CI gate; spec-reviewer **0 blocker / 0 major** + Codex **0 defects**. **M3:** the fresh spec-reviewer's **blocker** (percentile → 1e9-grid round-down), **major** (decision vectors → standalone-replayable) and per-gate-veto-order minor fixed; welfare pipeline now grid-exact end-to-end. **M1:** `Proposal`(21-field)/`ExecutionRecord`/`MarketSet`/`MarketKind`/`phase_offsets` single-homed in `futarchy-primitives`; `wt.quorum` double-copy + ~14 core constant duplications collapsed; `MaxEncodedLen`/golden-order/view-size regression tests; spec-reviewer major + all actionable minors fixed. **Also:** 15 §4.4 MPFR wording clarified (≥256-bit; the model's 100-digit `Decimal` ≈ 332-bit satisfies it) and the stale `.claude/rules/reference-model.md` re-trued (corpus schema owned by 04 §5). **Open follow-ups:** the ≥10⁷ MPFR sweep + supply-chain CI legs are B8; new **SQ-39…SQ-43** (08 §4.1 nav-floor rounding, `sec.prize.*` default, 04 §7 clamp-k, 05 §4.4 C_daily weight grid, `CohortSummary` bound) await a future 02/05/08 touch — **SQ-44** (`MarketKind` variant spelling) was **resolved** this session by conforming the code to 02 §5's canonical `GateS_Adopt`/… names (PR #49 rebased onto A2/#48 + Codex-comment triage).

**Track A COMPLETE — A1–A11 are all production `#[frame_support::pallet]`s ✅ (A8 + A11 landed 2026-07-16, by Codex subagents at gpt-5.6-sol/xhigh).** Each has a relocated frame-free functional core in `crates/<name>-core/` and a FRAME shell over it (bounded storage matching 02 byte-for-byte, origin-checked extrinsics, try-state hooks, benchmarks/weights, Doc-15 suites). **A5 (`pallet-oracle`) carried the 02 §7.2 contract reconciliation (triple key, `INTEGRATION_CONTRACT_VERSION` 2→3) early to break the A5 → B2 → B1a → A1–A11 circular dependency.** **A8 (`pallet-epoch`)** = the epoch/phase clock + T1–T24 proposal machine + the 11-step `decide()` engine + cohorts + `RecentCohortSummaries` ring. **A11 (`pallet-execution-guard`, audit-scope-A/R-7)** = the queue + permissionless atomic `execute()` (13-item dispatch, class origins, internal Root only for `authorize_upgrade`) + two-phase upgrade + `DescriptorLeadTime` + the A8↔A11 `dequeue_terminal` cleanup handoff. **B1a runtime assembly is now unblocked** — it owns `construct_runtime!` + wiring every Track-A seam (the guard's `Dispatcher`/SafetyFilter/attestor/epoch seams, the best-effort-wrapper rejection SQ-96, the class-origin `RuntimeCall` projection); B2–B6 follow.

**A7 ✅ (2026-07-16).** `pallets/welfare` is a production `#[frame_support::pallet]` over `welfare-core`: three **02 §7.4-frozen** `StorageMap`s (`MetricSpecs`/`Snapshots`/`GateBreachFlags`; `GateBreachFlags: map EpochId→flags` per 05 §4.7) via a scoped `load`(sorted)→core→`checked` `persist` adapter; a **rule-4 Params consumer** (θS/θC lo/hi + wP/wA from `pallet-constitution::Params`, threaded into a behavior-preserving core `WelfareParams`); `register_spec` (ConstitutionalValues) + `record_snapshot`/`record_daily_gate` (Signed keeper cranks, activation-checked) + the internal SettleAuthority `compute_settlement` (05 §6, `with_storage_layer`-atomic, class-gated `settle_gate`) + `prune` (rolling-20 reap). Orchestrated with **Codex subagents** (author → dual review → fix → regression pass): the dual review's 1 blocker + 6 majors (storage-shape→maps, no-pruning→reap, MetricSpec validation, settlement atomicity, inactive-spec, seam versioning, class-gated gates) + a regression minor all fixed in-session with tests; final Codex review **0 blocker/0 major**. On the PR the **Codex-connector** flagged **2 more**, both fixed: **P1** — the keeper cranks accepted an unfinalized/future `epoch`, so an early call could lock a wrong `W` or consume the bounded window before the counters exist; a pallet `epoch < CurrentEpoch` guard (`EpochNotFinalized`, 05 §4.6 finalized-epoch rule) now rejects them. **P2** — genesis specs were forced to `activation ≥ 2`, so `record_snapshot(1, …)` was rejected and W₁ was uncomputable; genesis registration (epoch-0 sentinel) now activates at epoch 1 (05 §4.6 cold start; the two-epoch lead only guards post-genesis version changes). R-1: 06 §3.2 keeper-crank rows added; SQ-77…82 logged. Gates green (workspace 498; welfare 32 pallet + 18 core). **Next: A8/A11 per the Track-A DoD, then B1a** (which wires the welfare `MetricInputs`/`Ledger` seams + epoch-driven snapshot/prune/settlement triggers + the I-16 cohort→spec_version binding).

**A3 ✅ (2026-07-15).** `pallets/market` is a production `#[frame_support::pallet]` over `market-core`: `Markets` (`CountedStorageMap`, 196-cap enforced at dispatch) + `BaselineMarketOf` (02 §7.4), the frozen 02 §5 event set, `buy`/`sell`/`crank_observe`/`reap` (Signed) + internal `create_market`/`seed`/`close` (`MarketAdmin`), a `LedgerOps` shim driving the real `pallet-conditional-ledger` `do_*` API (the market *is* the ledger's `MarketAuthority`; atomicity via `with_storage_layer`), live `mkt.fee`/`obs_interval`/`kappa` via Config, seed idempotency, and a `try_state` covering I-12 structural collateralization + I-13 accumulator sanity. The `market-core` refactor (`LedgerOps` trait + `MarketParams` + `buy_book`/`sell_book`/`seed_book`/`observe_book`) is behavior-identical at default params (differential preserved). Implemented by a **Codex background task** to a 6-phase brief, then dual-reviewed (adversarial `codex exec` + `spec-reviewer`) and hardened (`test-engineer`); both reviews' blockers were fixed with regression tests — **multi-book proposals shared one vault** (create was per-book) and **Baseline sells charged the seller** (the seller funded their own payout against the real ledger; the book now funds it) — plus the crank/196-cap/seed-idempotency/try-state majors, and the **PR #53 Codex-bot P1s** (Baseline seeding funded from `treasury` not the book; internal `seed`/`create_market` wrapped in `with_storage_layer`). Deferred by design: **SQ-64**–**SQ-67** and the A8 (TWAP window/checkpoints, settlement-anchored reap) / B1a (`create_market` epoch/spec params, deterministic book/fee sub-accounts, `Params` binding) items. ### Track A — Protocol pallets

**Re-scoped 2026-07-14 (user-directed; see Decision log): Track A delivers production
Polkadot-SDK FRAME pallets, not frame-free models. A1–A11 are reopened ⬜.** Their logic
already exists as **frame-free functional-core models** (state struct + `fn op(&mut self)
-> Result` + typed Event/Error + `try_state`); that code is **kept as the functional
core**, relocated to `crates/<name>-core/` (`no_std`, no `frame` deps — rule 9 / 01 §5.2),
and preserved as the differential oracle (Python M3 ≡ Rust core ≡ FRAME runtime) and the
WASM-portable / auditor-consumable port. A milestone is ✅ only once its pallet ships in
full FRAME production style — the **necessary parts** per pallet:

- **`crates/<name>-core/`** — the relocated frame-free model (functional core; today's
  `pallets/<name>` logic, unchanged in behavior).
- **`pallets/<name>/src/lib.rs`** — a `#[frame_support::pallet]` shell: a `Config` trait
  (`RuntimeEvent`, `WeightInfo`, constants via `Get<…>`, `Params`/currency/asset + origin
  bounds); `#[pallet::storage]` items as `BoundedVec`/`BoundedBTreeMap` (`MaxEncodedLen`,
  bounds from 13 §4, names + SCALE shapes matching 02 byte-for-byte — rule 5);
  `#[pallet::event]` / `#[pallet::error]` mapped 1:1 from the core; `#[pallet::call]`
  extrinsics that enforce an explicit origin (`EnsureOrigin` over `pallet-origins`, one
  SafetyFilter authority-matrix row per call — 06 §3) then load storage → call the core →
  persist → deposit events, each carrying `#[pallet::weight(T::WeightInfo::…)]`;
  `#[pallet::hooks]` with the mandatory `try_state` (15 §1) and only the cursor-bounded
  cranks the spec allows (none where it says none — the ledger has no hooks, 03 §10);
  `#[pallet::genesis_config]` / `genesis_build` where the pallet has genesis state.
- **`pallets/<name>/src/mock.rs`** — a mock runtime (`construct_runtime!`: `System` + the
  pallet + its dependencies, with test `Config` impls).
- **`pallets/<name>/src/tests.rs`** — per-extrinsic × error-path × origin-misuse tests
  through the closed wrapper set, limit/boundary coverage, and a `try_state` assertion
  (15 §4.1, §1). Audit-scope-A pallets (A1, A2, A11 — R-7) add the adversarial /
  rounding-against-the-claimant / solvency suites.
- **`pallets/<name>/src/benchmarking.rs`** + **`weights.rs`** — `#[benchmarks]` for every
  extrinsic and hook, a `WeightInfo` trait, a generated `weights.rs`, and the
  `runtime-benchmarks` feature. PoV-calibrated weights land with B5; the harness + stubs
  are part of the milestone.
- **`Cargo.toml`** — `frame-support` / `frame-system` / `frame-benchmarking` on the
  `polkadot-stable2603` pins (01 §9), the `std` / `runtime-benchmarks` / `try-runtime`
  features, and the `<name>-core` dependency.

Scaffold via `/new-pallet` (already emits this shape); `test-engineer` authors the 15 §4
suites; a `spec-reviewer` pass with no blockers precedes ✅ (R-6). Per-pallet FRAME wrapping
lives here; runtime-level `construct_runtime!` / `impl_runtime_apis!` assembly is B1a/B2.

a `RebatePayout` seam paying real USDC from the `bl/trsry`-derived `KEEPER__`/`ORACLE__` pots (payout-first, meter/line commit only on success; `pot_balance` feeds the new try-state **custody-drift alarm** line ≤ pot, SQ-123); `TreasuryParams` gains `keeper_budget_epoch` + fail-soft-0 `keeper_rebate` (unseeded by design, SQ-117). **Rebate call sites in every crank pallet, strictly state-advancing** (no-op cranks never pay — R-7 drain-vector protection): epoch `tick`/`decide`(None→Some + latch-once extension)/`settle_cohort` (DecisionCritical); market `crank_observe` (recorded-only; DecisionCritical via the `InDecisionWindow` seam, pending-false → General until A8 wiring, SQ-118)/`reap`; welfare `record_snapshot` (DecisionCritical)/`record_daily_gate` (**state-change-gated** — identical re-records pay zero, SQ-122); ledger sweeps (positive residual, advancing partial batches, zero-residue full reap); guard `execute` (terminal dequeue only; `reap_prequeue_ratification` deliberately unrebated); oracle `crank_round_close` (terminal + latch-once extension)/`crank_reserve_probe` (**gated on `ProbeDispatch::live()`** — the pending `()` dispatcher pays nothing)/`recompute_proof`/`ack_observed` (07 §4, OracleLine, SQ-121); registry `crank_close` (**favorable closures only — an all-quorum-failure rejection batch pays zero**, killing the file→refund→close farm; challenge-resolved rejections also unpaid = conservative under-rebate)/`reap_epoch`/`ack_observed` — oracle/registry from the oracle line (SQ-116), unlisted cranks General (SQ-115). Runtime binds every wired pallet + the ForeignAssets payout adapter; epoch/guard seams bind at the open A8/A11 wiring (pending epoch-0 clock = one un-resetting budget, conservative). **Off-chain:** `keeper/bleavit-keeper` — a **separate cargo workspace** (subxt 0.44 tree isolated from the `=`-exact stable2603 pins; root `exclude` + own CI gate leg) — subxt-**dynamic** transport (no codegen; absent pallets = capability-disabled roles), pure unit-tested planner over finalized-head snapshots (due-predicates mirror the on-chain guards; decision-critical priority incl. stale-decision-window escalation; per-crank cooldowns; zero-filing epochs deliberately never planned — the A6 `FilingCount` ruling), nonce-pipelined race-tolerant submitter, per-role Prometheus metrics for the 12 §6.3 RB-KEEPER rows, dry-run mode, **live mode refuses to start without an explicit signer**, operator README. **Orchestrated with Codex subagents (gpt-5.6-sol/xhigh)**: 2 parallel authors → triple review (spec-reviewer ×2: on-chain 0/2/4, off-chain 0/1/5 + adversarial Codex 2 blockers/4 majors/2 minors) → 2 fix rounds (9 on-chain + 6 keeper fixes, every finding closed or logged) → 1 surgical revert (the off-chain review's empty-epoch major was wrong at the pallet layer — A6's deliberate `FilingCount` guard) → fix-round internal re-review 0/0 + orchestrator spot-verification. SQ-115…SQ-126 logged. Gates green (workspace + keeper workspace + benchmarks + try-runtime + no_std + reference-model + doc links). **Follow-ups:** weights recalibration incl. registry `WeightInfo=()` (B5); custody funding-sync mechanism (SQ-123); `InDecisionWindow`/epoch-clock live bindings (A8 wiring); RB-KEEPER runbook (O4) |

## Spec questions

Open ambiguities/contradictions found in `docs/architecture/`. Record them here first;
under rule R-1 a genuine defect may be corrected in the spec directly, but log
non-obvious semantic changes and confirm with the user before diverging.
Format: `| ID | Question | Spec ref | Raised | Status |`

| ID | Question | Spec ref | Raised | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| SQ-119 | 08 §1.4's event list writes fields where they exist (`KeeperBudgetExhausted { epoch, spent }`) but lists `KeeperBudgetLow` bare; A9 declared (and B9 emits) `KeeperBudgetLow { remaining: Balance }`. Does the bare listing freeze a field-less event, or may it carry the diagnostic payload? Keep `remaining` (useful, pre-existing A9 surface, 02 freezes neither keeper event) and amend 08 §1.4 at the next 08 touch, or drop the field? | 08 §1.4, §6.3 | 2026-07-16 (B9 spec-review) | open — `remaining` kept (pre-genesis, no consumer breakage possible); needs the 08 §1.4 wording ratified |
| SQ-120 | 08 §6.3 "100% ⇒ `KeeperBudgetExhausted`… rebates stop": a literal 100% trigger never fires unless spend lands exactly on the budget (budget rarely an exact multiple of `keeper.rebate`). B9 implements **effective exhaustion** — the first unpayable attempt emits the event (degenerately `{spent: 0}` when `rebate > budget` on a fresh meter, e.g. after a governance shrink) — **plus a payment latch**: once emitted, rebates stay off for the rest of the epoch even if a mid-epoch `keeper.rebate` reduction would fit again. Ratify both readings. | 08 §6.3 | 2026-07-16 (B9 dual review) | open — effective-exhaustion + latch implemented (loud + conservative); ratify or refine at the next 08 touch |
| SQ-121 | 07 §4 mandates a "keeper-class fee rebate" for watchtower `ack_observed`; B9 pays it from the **oracle budget line** (`CrankClass::OracleLine`, consistent with SQ-116's routing) in **both** the oracle pallet and the registry instances — though 07 §7's registry call table does not restate the rebate for the registry's ack. Confirm the routing and the registry-instance applicability. | 07 §4, §7 | 2026-07-16 (B9 dual review) | open — implemented OracleLine on both (dedup-guarded, drain-safe) |
| SQ-122 | 05 §4.7 is silent on `record_daily_gate` cardinality: the extrinsic is repeat-tolerant (a duplicate `(epoch, day, spec_version)` OR-merges identical flags — a state no-op). B9 keeps it repeat-tolerant but rebates only recordings that actually change state (first write of the day, or genuinely new flags), closing the general-tranche drain both reviews flagged. Should duplicates instead be rejected outright on-chain? | 05 §4.7; 08 §6.3; R-7 | 2026-07-16 (B9 dual review) | open — repeat-tolerant + state-change-gated rebate implemented; per the PR #62 bot P2 the duplicate detector moved off the frozen breach bitmap onto the internal `SampledGateDays` marker (breach bitmap = breached days only again) |
| SQ-123 | Treasury custody sync: `fund_budget_line` moves value only inside the internal line ledger, while B9's rebate payouts transfer real USDC from the `KEEPER__`/`ORACLE__` `bl/trsry` sub-account pots — nothing moves custody when a line is funded, so line-ledger vs pot balances can drift (funded line + empty pot = every payout silently skipped; funded pot + empty line = stranded funds). B9 adds the loud alarm (try-state: per payout line, internal balance ≤ pot balance) but NOT the sync mechanism — which is the A9 "asset custody / fungibles" follow-up. Where does custody sync live (fund_budget_line moving USDC between sub-accounts, or a genesis/ops funding convention)? | 08 §1.1, §6; A9 follow-ups | 2026-07-16 (B9 Codex adversarial) | open — drift alarm shipped; sync mechanism owned by the treasury-custody follow-up (B1a/B4 scope) |
| SQ-124 | 12 §6.3's keeper inactivity row ("no crank 1 h") doesn't say whether the signal is chain-observed (rebate/extrinsic events) or daemon-side, nor how to avoid false positives when a role legitimately has no due work for >1 h (no trading books d18–d21; capability-disabled roles on the current runtime). The reference keeper ships per-role metrics + last-success timestamps and the README recommends a `for: 1h` guard excluding disabled roles. Pin the intended semantics at the next 12 touch. | 12 §6.3 | 2026-07-16 (B9 off-chain spec-review) | open — daemon-side per-role metrics implemented |
| SQ-125 | 13 §3.1 mandates that clients bind the phase fractions via pallet metadata constants, but `pallet-epoch` exposes no phase-fraction constants (`extra_constants` has only the contract version/bounds/`TickBatch`) — so neither the keeper nor the future FE has a compliant binding path and both must mirror the kernel grid in code. Confirm the queued B2 contract amendment adds the actual metadata-constant exposure to `pallet-epoch`. | 13 §3.1; 02 (B2 amendment queue) | 2026-07-16 (B9 off-chain spec-review) | open — keeper mirrors the grid with a documented note until the constants exist |
| SQ-126 | No spec text defines the off-chain keeper's parameter-sourcing obligation: must it track live `Constitution.Params` values (`mkt.obs_interval`, `dec.window`, `res.probe_*`), or may it ship normative defaults with operator overrides (as the reference implementation does, dynamic `ParamValue` decoding being unspecified for clients)? | 01 §4.2; 12 §6.1; 13 §1 | 2026-07-16 (B9 off-chain spec-review) | open — narrowed by the PR #62 bot P1: the keeper now resolves `mkt.obs_interval`, `dec.window`, `res.probe_int`, `res.probe_to` from live `Constitution.Params` (override > live > documented default); the residual question is only whether live-tracking is *mandatory* for clients |
| SQ-115 | 08 §6.3's decision-critical tranche list ("decision-window observations, `decide`, `settle_cohort`, `tick`, `snapshot`") is treated as exhaustive by B9, so the unlisted keeper cranks — `welfare.record_daily_gate` (a decision *input*, 05 §4.7), `execution_guard.execute`/`reap_prequeue_ratification` (01 §4.2 names "execution" a keeper crank; arguably decision-critical since it finalizes an adopted decision), `futarchy_treasury.execute_coretime_renewal` (09 §4 "keeper-rebated"), and every reap/dust crank — rebate from the ≤20% **General** tranche. Conservative for the reserved tranche, but confirm none of these belongs in the ≥80% decision-critical reservation. | 08 §6.3; 01 §4.2; 05 §4.7; 09 §4 | 2026-07-16 (B9) | open — General implemented for all unlisted cranks; reclassification is a one-line class change per call site |
| SQ-116 | 07 §7's registry cranks (`crank_close` "Signed (keeper, rebated)", `reap_epoch`) name no funding line. B9 routes them through the **oracle budget line** (unmetered by the 08 §6.3 keeper meter), by analogy with 07's pallet-table row pinning `crank_round_close`/probe cranks to the oracle line — the registry is a 07-owned component. Confirm, or assign them to the KEEPER meter. | 07 §7; 07 pallet table; 08 §6.3 | 2026-07-16 (B9) | open — oracle-line routing implemented behind the same `CrankClass::OracleLine` path |

Where does the value get seeded: a B5 post-benchmark 13 §1 edit (hypothesis default per 13 rule 4) or a runtime `amend_registry` after launch? Until then A-1's "rebated" incentive is inert (ops-line keepers only). | 13 §1 (`keeper.rebate`); 08 §6.2; B5 | 2026-07-16 (B9) | open — fail-soft-0 implemented (cannot create unbacked outflow); needs the B5 fee-basis [VERIFY] resolution |
| SQ-118 | 08 §6.3's "decision-window observations" classification needs the owning pair's decision window (final 72 h, `dec.window`), which `pallet-market` does not own — the window is epoch/proposal state (05/A8). B9 adds an `InDecisionWindow` Config seam to `pallet-market`; the runtime binds a pending **always-false** adapter (⇒ every observation rebates as General) until the open B1a A8 wiring lands and `pallet-epoch` can answer it. Conservative for the reserved tranche but under-rebates the decision-critical observation load (the 20% general cap starves observation rebates at scale). Bind with the A8 runtime wiring. | 08 §6.3; 04 §7; 05 §2 | 2026-07-16 (B9) | open — pending-false adapter wired; the A8 runtime-wiring follow-up owns the real binding |
| SQ-109 | **Ratify two B3 genesis-economics rulings** made under the session's standing delegation (both conservative, both spec-pinned in the amended 08 §2.1): (a) founding-team vesting = the **0%-at-cliff** single-schedule curve (not the conventional 25% catch-up — see the 2026-07-16 Decision-log row for why catch-up is unsafe at genesis); (b) **unvested VIT cannot pay transaction fees** (strict "nothing spendable before the cliff"; founding-team accounts pay fees in USDC per 08 §9 — a reviewed-then-removed fee carve-out adapter is preserved in git history if the ruling is reversed). | 08 §2.1, §9; D-15 | 2026-07-16 (B3 dual review) | open — rulings live in code + spec text; reverse-able pre-genesis at zero migration cost |

Candidate mechanisms: a treasury-pallet VIT-stream analog, plain scheduled transfers under a distribution pallet/call, or a spec'd runtime-internal dispatch. | 08 §2.1; 01 §5.1; D-13 | 2026-07-16 (B3 spec-reviewer) | open — owns no code today (distribution is a Phase-4-adjacent milestone); must be resolved before Phase-4 arming |
| SQ-108 | **Should the treasury pot-account derivations be contract-frozen?** B3 pins MAIN = `PalletId(*b"bl/trsry").into_account_truncating()`, community/incentives = sub-seeds `communty`/`incentiv`; the deploy template + validator hardcode the resulting ss58-7777 addresses. 08 §1.1 names the sub-accounts but pins no derivation; if the FE/operators/auditors must recompute these, 13 §3.5 (or 02 §8, with a contract bump) should freeze the derivation. | 08 §1.1; 13 §3.5; 02 §8 | 2026-07-16 (B3 spec-reviewer) | open — freeze at the next 02/13 touch (B2 or B4) |
| SQ-105 | **(bot P1) Phase-3 real-USDC exposure caps not enforced on ledger inflows.** `phase3.tvl_cap`/`phase3.deposit_cap` (D-13) live in the constitution registry but nothing consumes them: once B4 supplies real USDC and vault creation is live, a signed user could split/credit USDC with no global or per-account cap check, removing D-13's bound on sudo-era exposure. **Scope:** 09 §5.2 enforces the caps "at every split/inflow-crediting path **and** the XCM inflow leg" — the split path is `pallet-conditional-ledger` (A2) and the inflow leg is B4; **neither is runtime-`Config` wiring** (per-account cumulative-deposit accounting is ledger storage). | SQ-106 | 02 §3/§4 spell the API collection bounds as FRAME's `BoundedVec<T, ConstU32<N>>`, but 02 §2 + rule 9 / 01 §5.2 require every view type to live in the frame-free `futarchy-primitives`, whose `BoundedVec<T, const N: u32>` cannot take the sp type — the spec's spelling and the crate-layering rule are in literal tension. De-facto accepted since M1 (all Track-A pallets + the B2 `FutarchyApi` declaration use the primitives type); wire-format equality with `bounded_collections::BoundedVec<T, ConstU32<N>>` is now pinned both directions by `api_collections_encode_identically_to_frame_bounded_vec` (runtime-api). Residual: the **TypeInfo/metadata shape** differs (derived composite vs FRAME's sequence-like info), which generated frontend descriptors will surface — B1a's `impl_runtime_apis!` golden-metadata test must decide whether to keep the composite shape (and bless it in 02 §3's wording) or hand-implement a sequence `TypeInfo`. | 02 §3–§4; 01 §5.2; rule 9 | 2026-07-16 (B2 spec-review + Codex adversarial) | open — encoding pinned identical by test; metadata-shape decision lands with B1a's golden runtime-API metadata test; 02 wording clarified at the next 02 touch |
| SQ-104 | `authorize_upgrade` domain vs matrix, and the migration/xcmp/collator Root-admin surface. B1a projects `system.authorize_upgrade` → `InternalRoot` (denied for every origin incl. `FutarchyCode`, contradicting 06 §3.2 row 3's FutarchyCode ✔) because its dispatch is guard-internal Root (I-10, 09 §2.1(3)); and it classifies migrations `force_*`/xcmp admin/collator `set_*` as `Public` (Root-gated in-pallet → sudo-reachable bootstrap admin), but 06 §6.2 assigns migration-cursor control to the **EmergencyPlaybook** set, which would fail `ensure_root` in-pallet — the PB-MIGRATION lane needs an origin bridge. Also: how is the Phase-3→4 upgrade authorized while the guard (A11) is absent, given 09 §5.3 gives sudo that power but the InternalRoot projection denies it? Overlaps main's SQ-93 (A11 apply-mechanism). | 06 §3.2 row 3, §6.2; 09 §2.1(3)/§5.3; I-10 | 2026-07-16 (B1a dual review) | open — A11-wiring/B6: `authorize_upgrade` admissibility must not rest on the interim InternalRoot denial; plan the migrations→EmergencyPlaybook origin bridge. | SQ-103 | **(bot P1) Values referenda track collapse + track-config code home.** Stock `pallet-referenda` selects the track from the proposal origin (`track_for`), so the five 06 §2.1 tracks that all produce `ConstitutionalValues` (metric/constitution/entrenched/guardian/ratify) cannot be discriminated — collapsing them onto one track ID would let an entrenched-scope action (e.g. lowering the entrenched-class `att.bond`) enact at a weaker track's threshold. **B1a fix:** the single shared `ConstitutionalValues` track now uses the **strongest (entrenched) thresholds** — 80% approval, 20%→10% support, 50,000-VIT deposit, 4-epoch-equivalent (7 d/28 d/7 d, 28 d enactment) — so **no values action can enact below its required bar** (over-strict but G-1-safe); `OracleResolution` keeps its own track (60% / 10%→3% / 7 d). | SQ-32 | 06 §3.3's two-check model — "(b) `BaseCallFilter` **denies governance-privileged calls unless dispatched with their matching custom origin** — enforced again by each pallet's `EnsureOrigin`" — cannot be realized inside a `Contains<RuntimeCall>`, which is origin-blind. The implemented split (A4): the **origin-less** base filter denies the nobody row, the dangerous wrappers, and bare governance leaves (a signed submitter carries no matching custom origin); the **origin-aware** re-check (`SafetyFilter::validate(Some(origin), …)`, already applied by `execution-guard-core` at execute, I-11) plus each pallet's `EnsureOrigin` runs at the governance dispatch boundary (guard; scheduler per §3.4), which then dispatches via `dispatch_bypass_filter`. This is safe/conservative and matches the guard core, but 06 §3.3's `impl Contains` reference block (`_ => static_domain_allowed(c)`) reads ambiguously — the A4 Codex adversarial review reads it as *allowing* bare governance leaves at the base filter (origin enforced solely by `EnsureOrigin`), and warns that naïvely setting `BaseCallFilter = SafetyFilter` on the enactment path would `BadOrigin`-reject every custom-origin call and stall governance. Should 06 §3.3 be clarified to state explicitly that (i) the origin-less `BaseCallFilter` denies bare governance-privileged leaves and (ii) governance/scheduler enactment bypasses it and re-validates origin-aware — pinning the B1a wiring? Code is internally consistent under the conservative reading; this is a spec-clarity + B1a-wiring item, not a current safety defect. | 06 §3.3(b)/§3.4; 09 §1.2 (guard) | 2026-07-15 (A4 Codex review) | open |
| SQ-31 | 06 §3.3's `MAX_NESTED` "≤ 16 calls total" bound is ambiguous in scope. The core's global-node reading is the conservative, G-1-safe one but may over-reject a legitimate maximal batch. | SQ-3 | `AttestationMissing` has two mandated producing sites across the doc set, which 05's exclusivity clause forbids. 05 §1.3 declares "every variant has exactly one producing site … MUST NOT emit from any other site" and maps `AttestationMissing` to `decide()` step 10 → T10; 05 §2.1 T16 enumerates the `Queued → Rejected` reason set as `{ StaleQueue, NotRatified }` only. The A11 (#40) fix implements the 09/I-19 behavior (guard propagates `AttestationMissing` through `epoch.expire_or_stale_queue` → T16-shaped reject → T21), so it is compliant with the execution guard's owning doc but violates 05's producer-map exclusivity and T16's closed reason set. **Recommended resolution:** extend 05 §2.1 T16's reason set to include `AttestationMissing` and relax 05 §1.3's "exactly one producing site" clause for this variant (option a) — dropping the dispatch-time producer (option b) would remove a security check (I-19). Needs a spec decision, not a code change; the code already tracks 09. | 05 §1.3, §2.1 T16 vs 09 §1.2(5); 15 I-19 | 2026-07-14 | **resolved 2026-07-14** (option a, user-approved; 05 §1.3/§2.1 + 15 I-19 edited — see Decision log) |
| SQ-2 | 02 §7.2 pins `ComponentValues` as `map (MetricId, EpochId) → SettledComponent` (no version), but 07 §2(4) runs the reporting game per `(component, epoch, frozen spec version)` with one settlement per version across a MetricSpec activation boundary — the pair key cannot represent two per-version settled values. `pallet-oracle` (PR #30 follow-up) now keys rounds/settled values by the triple; the 02 contract row needs a resolution at the B2 mapping (append a versioned map or key change — requires the joint backend+frontend sign-off and a contract-version bump per 02 §13). **The same B2 amendment batch also carries three more 02 reconciliations surfaced by the #46 Codex review (2026-07-15)** — (a) the 02 §9 intake-row erratum (binding target for `intake.max_per_account` is `params()` + K-bound metadata constants, not a "≤ 4" metadata constant — SQ-23); (b) splitting 02 §9's combined `epoch.length`/`epoch.slots`/phase-offset-fractions row so the fractions bind via metadata constants only (13 §3.1 resolution, SQ-24); (c) adding the `pallet-attestor` storage/view shape to 02 §7 (referenced by 01 §5.1 and 06 §7; read by the FE on the CODE/META execute path, SQ-26) — so the contract version bumps once. | 02 §7.2; 07 §2(4) | 2026-07-14 | **oracle portion resolved 2026-07-15 (contract v3, see [SQ-58]);** the remaining three batch items — (a) intake-row erratum (SQ-23), (b) phase-offset row split (SQ-24), (c) `pallet-attestor` 02 §7 row (SQ-26) — still ride a **later** bump when their surfaces are next touched. ## Decision log

Spec changes and other project decisions (rule R-1, AGENTS.md).

| Date | Amendment | Authorized by | Docs touched |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2026-07-16 | **B4 re-review clarifications in 09 (teleport scope + renewal route shape).** (a) §6.1's "teleports disabled" row gained its scope: the prohibition binds *this chain's executor* (`IsTeleporter = ()` inbound and outbound) — it does not forbid programs this chain authors from instructing the **relay** to run its canonical DOT teleport to a system chain, which executes on the relay under the relay's own trust rules and creates no teleport trust here (the re-review's spec question; narrow reading adopted — the wide reading would make the 09 §4 renewal transfer impossible, since the Coretime chain accepts DOT **only** as a relay teleport, V-18). (b) §4's renewal sentence now names the verified two-leg route (local reserve-withdraw → relay `InitiateTeleport` → Coretime), replacing the reserve-transfer wording that the live Coretime config would reject (`IsReserve = ()`, `UntrustedReserveLocation`). | Session decision under R-1 (live-config contradiction proven, V-18; conservative: no new trust surface on this chain), user standing delegation this session | 09, PLAN.md |
| 2026-07-16 | **B4 review-driven 09 §6.1 amendment + 13 §3.5 additions.** (a) The trapped-assets row's "recovery via a TREASURY-class `claim_assets` call only" was **unimplementable**: stable2603's `AssetTrap` keys every trap by the origin that dropped the assets and `pallet_xcm::claim_assets` derives the claim key from the caller — a TREASURY origin can never match user- or remote-keyed traps, so all non-treasury traps would have been permanently stranded (B4 adversarial review, blocker 7). Amended to **self-scoped recovery**: Signed accounts reclaim only traps keyed to their own origin (no new authority — self-scoping is enforced by the trap-key mechanism itself), TREASURY-class for protocol-keyed traps, remote-keyed traps only via an inbound `ClaimAsset` program, and the §5.2 caps moved to the *mint* leg as the upstream mitigation. (b) 13 §3.5 gained the counterparty-system-chain row (Asset Hub 1000, **Coretime 1005** — V-17) giving `CORETIME_PARA_ID` its spec home, and its USDC row's `[VERIFY asset index 1337]` cleared per V-16 (13 is not the contract — no bump). | 2026-07-14 | A11 (review fix) | Fixed the five Codex findings on PR #40 (`pallet-execution-guard`), traced to 09/05/13: **(P1) preimage binding** — `execute`/`check_dispatch_time` now re-derive the payload hash from the SCALE-encoded calls (`hash_payload`, excluding the model's runtime-outcome `succeeds`/`error` fields) and match it against the committed `payload_hash`, so a keeper can no longer swap `payload.calls` under the queued hash (09 §1.2(2)). **(P1) apply-upgrade verification** — `apply_authorized_upgrade` now takes the artifact bytes, re-derives the hash via `content_hash` (not a trusted caller field), and records the *authorized* `target_spec_version`, rejecting a spoofed `observed_spec_version` (`UpgradeVersionMismatch`) (09 §2.1(4)/(6)). **(P1) T18/T22/T23 failure path** — a reverted batch now advances the epoch proposal `Queued → FailedExecuted` (new `pallet-epoch::mark_failed_executed`, event `ExecutionFailed{PayloadReverted}`), writes the failure record, keeps the queue entry retryable within `RETRY_WINDOW` (72 h), returns `Ok` so the transition persists; a successful retry runs T23 via `mark_executed`, and `expire_failed_execution` drives T22 (`retry_exhausted_to_measurement`, resolve-Accept → Measuring) once the window closes (05 §2.1 T18/T22/T23). **(P2) AttestationMissing propagation** — `pallet-epoch::expire_or_stale_queue` now handles `AttestationMissing` (T16→T21) and the guard propagates the epoch result instead of discarding it, so a dispatch-time attestation revocation no longer strands the proposal `Queued` (09 §1.2(5)). **(P2) META upgrades** — `domain_allowed` admits the internal-root authorize/apply domains for CODE **or** META (09 §2). Six regression tests added (one per finding + existing suite updated); full Rust workspace gates, execution-guard/epoch no-default-features and runtime-benchmarks tests, docs link lint, and the reference-model suite green. A `spec-reviewer` pass over both files vs 09 §1–§3 / 05 §2.1 / 13 / 15 I-9/I-10/I-11/I-19 confirmed all five fixes compliant with their owning docs (0 blocker / 0 major); it surfaced **SQ-3** — `AttestationMissing` is mandated as a dispatch-time reject reason by 09 §1.2(5)/I-19 but was forbidden by 05 §1.3's single-producer clause and T16's closed reason set (the code tracks 09). **SQ-3 resolved this same session (option a, user-approved):** 05 §1.3/§2.1 and 15 I-19 edited to make `AttestationMissing` a deliberately dual-sited reason (T10 decide-time + T16 dispatch-time re-check); no `RejectReason` variant added, so 02 is untouched and no contract bump is needed (see Decision log). Two minor model-fidelity notes (T22 `PayloadReverted` not annotated onto a cohort `DecisionRecord` — this model has none; `apply_authorized_upgrade` records the authorized target rather than the literal "observed" version — intentional hardening, behaviorally equal on the honest path) accepted as-is. A11 remains ✅. | B1 — Runtime assembly |

| 2026-07-15 | A2 (#48 Codex review triage, autonomous) | Triaged the three `chatgpt-codex-connector` findings on PR #48 (`pallet-conditional-ledger`). **P1 (transactional wrapping) — FALSE POSITIVE, no fix:** Codex claimed FRAME dispatchables aren't rolled back on error unless `#[transactional]`. Not true for this SDK — frame-support 46.0.1's `#[pallet::call]` macro doc (`frame/support/src/lib.rs`) states every extrinsic is wrapped in `with_storage_layer`, so returning any error (incl. a late `T::Collateral::transfer` failure after `persist_*`) rolls the storage back; the pallet's module-doc + `reap_one` comment already rely on this (G-1). Strengthened the module-doc to name the mechanism so it isn't re-flagged. **P2 (transfer remainder sweep at the stale kernel floor) — TRUE, fixed:** 03 §7 R-2 binds the sweep to the LIVE `ledger.min_split` (a META tunable raisable to 1 USDC, 13 §1) but the core sweeps at the compile-time `kernel::MIN_TRANSFER_USDC` (0.01) and the pallet didn't override it, so once governance raises the tunable a Signed transfer could strand a sub-floor dust remainder. Added a pallet-level live-floor pre-sweep (bump `amount → balance` when the remainder would fall in `(0, MinSplit)`) before delegating; the core's K-floor sweep is then a no-op. Protocol senders exempt (exact by construction), matching the core. **P3 (`split_scalar`/`split_gate` skip the live creation floor) — TRUE, fixed:** R-2 "positions cannot be created below it" binds every Signed position-creating op, but only `split`/`split_baseline`/`transfer` enforced the live floor — the scalar/gate splits (which mint new LONG/SHORT/gate entries) delegated straight to the core, which guards no floor at all for them. Added `ensure!(amount >= T::MinSplit::get())` to both Signed extrinsics (the §5.1 rows omit it, but R-2 is the global rule; the `MarketAuthority` `do_*` paths stay exempt). Since `ledger.min_split`'s min IS the kernel floor (13 §1), the pallet check is always ≥ the core's, so no core/reference-model change needed. **Verification:** two regression tests (`scalar_and_gate_splits_enforce_live_min_split`, `transfer_remainder_sweep_uses_live_min_split`) drive the tunable to its 1-USDC ceiling via a now-`pub static MinSplit` mock param; confirmed both FAIL without the fixes (sweep left 0.5-USDC dust; sub-floor scalar split returned `Ok`) and pass with them. `differential_matches_frame_free_core` still green (pallet ≡ core at the default floor). | 2026-07-15 | A9 (PR #51 Codex-bot review round) | Addressed both `chatgpt-codex-connector` P2 comments on PR #51. **(1) Rolling issuance meter (resolves SQ-50 + SQ-54):** replaced the fixed-window `IssuanceMeter` (which reset `minted` at the 365-day boundary, letting a governance-timed `issue_vit` mint ≈2× `iss.inflation_cap` across the seam) with a bucketed **trailing 365-day `RollingMeter<366>`** — the same primitive as the 30d/180d outflow meters. `issue_vit` rolls a COPY (G-1 atomic), caps against `bps(vit_supply − trailing_minted, limit_bps)` (supply at window start) and commits on success; the trailing sum is never reset, so seam-straddling mints are summed and cannot exceed the cap. `try_state` now checks the trailing sum against the **fixed kernel ceiling** `ISS_INFLATION_CAP_BPS` (2%, down-only) rather than the live cap, so a mid-window down-amendment can't trigger a release-blocking failure (SQ-54).
